| pack\_‚Äãcomplete\_‚Äãmicroblock\_‚Äãduration\_‚Äãseconds | histogram | Duration of the computation associated with marking one microblock as complete |
| pack\_‚Äãtotal\_‚Äãtransactions\_‚Äãper\_‚Äãmicroblock\_‚Äãcount | histogram | Count of transactions in a scheduled microblock, including both votes and non-votes |
| pack\_‚Äãvotes\_‚Äãper\_‚Äãmicroblock\_‚Äãcount | histogram | Count of simple vote transactions in a scheduled microblock |
| pack\_‚Äãnormal\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãreceived | counter | Count of transactions received via the normal TPU path |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="instr\_‚Äãacct\_‚Äãcnt"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Transaction has an instruction that references too many accounts) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="nonce\_‚Äãconflict"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Bundle with two conflicting durable nonce transactions) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="bundle\_‚Äãblacklist"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Transaction uses an account on the bundle blacklist) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="invalid\_‚Äãnonce"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Transaction is an invalid durable nonce transaction) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="write\_‚Äãsysvar"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Transaction tries to write to a sysvar) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="estimation\_‚Äãfail"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Estimating compute cost and/or fee failed) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="duplicate\_‚Äãaccount"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Transaction included an account address twice) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="too\_‚Äãmany\_‚Äãaccounts"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Transaction tried to load too many accounts) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="too\_‚Äãlarge"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Transaction requests too many CUs) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="expired"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Transaction already expired) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="addr\_‚Äãlut"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Transaction loaded accounts from a lookup table) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="unaffordable"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Fee payer's balance below transaction fee) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="duplicate"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Pack aware of transaction with same signature) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="nonce\_‚Äãpriority"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Transaction's fee was too low given its compute unit requirement and another competing transactions that uses the same durable nonce) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="priority"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Transaction's fee was too low given its compute unit requirement and other competing transactions) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="nonvote\_‚Äãadd"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Transaction that was not a simple vote added to pending transactions) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="vote\_‚Äãadd"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Simple vote transaction was added to pending transactions) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="nonvote\_‚Äãreplace"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Transaction that was not a simple vote replaced a lower priority transaction) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="vote\_‚Äãreplace"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Simple vote transaction replaced a lower priority transaction) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="nonce\_‚Äãnonvote\_‚Äãadd"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Durable nonce transaction added to pending transactions) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="unused"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Unused because durable nonce transactions can't be simple votes) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãinsert\_‚Äãreturn="nonce\_‚Äãnonvote\_‚Äãreplace"} | counter | Result of inserting a transaction into the pack object (Durable nonce transaction replaced a lower priority transaction, likely one that uses the same durable nonce) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="no\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack had no transactions available, and wasn't leader) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="txn\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack had transactions available, but wasn't leader or had hit a limit) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="no\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack had no transactions available, had execle but wasn't leader) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="txn\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack had transactions available, had execle but wasn't leader) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="no\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack had no transactions available, and was leader but had no available execle) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="txn\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack had transactions available, was leader, but had no available execle) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="no\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack had available execle but no transactions) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="txn\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack had execle and transactions available but couldn't schedule anything non-conflicting) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="no\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack scheduled a non-empty microblock while not leader) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="txn\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack scheduled a non-empty microblock while not leader) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="no\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack scheduled a non-empty microblock while not leader) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="txn\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack scheduled a non-empty microblock while not leader) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="no\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack scheduled a non-empty microblock but all execle were busy) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="txn\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack scheduled a non-empty microblock but all execle were busy) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="no\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack scheduled a non-empty microblock and now has no transactions) |
| pack\_‚Äãmetric\_‚Äãtiming  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtiming\_‚Äãstate="txn\_‚Äãexecle\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãmicroblock"} | counter | Time in nanos spent in each state (Pack scheduled a non-empty microblock) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãdropped\_‚Äãfrom\_‚Äãextra | counter | Transactions dropped from the extra transaction storage because it was full |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted\_‚Äãto\_‚Äãextra | counter | Transactions inserted into the extra transaction storage because pack's primary storage was full |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãinserted\_‚Äãfrom\_‚Äãextra | counter | Transactions pulled from the extra transaction storage and inserted into pack's primary storage |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãexpired | counter | Transactions deleted from pack because their TTL expired |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãdeleted | counter | Transactions dropped from pack because they were requested to be deleted |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãalready\_‚Äãexecuted | counter | Transactions dropped from pack because they were already executed (in either the replay or leader pipeline) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãdropped\_‚Äãpartial\_‚Äãbundle | counter | Transactions dropped from pack because they were part of a partial bundle |
| pack\_‚Äãavailable\_‚Äãtransactions  <br>{avail\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãtype="all"} | gauge | The total number of pending transactions in pack's pool that are available to be scheduled (All transactions in any treap) |
| pack\_‚Äãavailable\_‚Äãtransactions  <br>{avail\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãtype="regular"} | gauge | The total number of pending transactions in pack's pool that are available to be scheduled (Non-votes in the main treap) |
| pack\_‚Äãavailable\_‚Äãtransactions  <br>{avail\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãtype="votes"} | gauge | The total number of pending transactions in pack's pool that are available to be scheduled (Simple votes) |
| pack\_‚Äãavailable\_‚Äãtransactions  <br>{avail\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãtype="conflicting"} | gauge | The total number of pending transactions in pack's pool that are available to be scheduled (Non-votes that write to a hotly-contended account) |
| pack\_‚Äãavailable\_‚Äãtransactions  <br>{avail\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãtype="bundles"} | gauge | The total number of pending transactions in pack's pool that are available to be scheduled (Transactions that are part of a bundle) |
| pack\_‚Äãpending\_‚Äãtransactions\_‚Äãheap\_‚Äãsize | gauge | The maximum number of pending transactions that pack can consider. This value is fixed at Firedancer startup but is a useful reference for AvailableTransactions |
| pack\_‚Äãsmallest\_‚Äãpending\_‚Äãtransaction | gauge | A lower bound on the smallest non-vote transaction (in cost units) that is immediately available for scheduling |
| pack\_‚Äãmicroblock\_‚Äãper\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãlimit | counter | The number of times pack did not pack a microblock because the limit on microblocks/block had been reached |
| pack\_‚Äãdata\_‚Äãper\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãlimit | counter | The number of times pack did not pack a microblock because it reached the data per block limit at the start of trying to schedule a microblock |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãschedule  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãschedule="taken"} | counter | Result of trying to consider a transaction for scheduling (Pack included the transaction in the microblock) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãschedule  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãschedule="cu\_‚Äãlimit"} | counter | Result of trying to consider a transaction for scheduling (Pack skipped the transaction because it would have exceeded the block CU limit) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãschedule  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãschedule="fast\_‚Äãpath"} | counter | Result of trying to consider a transaction for scheduling (Pack skipped the transaction because of account conflicts using the fast bitvector check) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãschedule  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãschedule="byte\_‚Äãlimit"} | counter | Result of trying to consider a transaction for scheduling (Pack skipped the transaction because it would have exceeded the block data size limit) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãschedule  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãschedule="alloc\_‚Äãlimit"} | counter | Result of trying to consider a transaction for scheduling (Pack skipped the transaction because it would have exceeded the data allocation limit) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãschedule  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãschedule="write\_‚Äãcost"} | counter | Result of trying to consider a transaction for scheduling (Pack skipped the transaction because it would have caused a writable account to exceed the per-account block write cost limit) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãschedule  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãschedule="slow\_‚Äãpath"} | counter | Result of trying to consider a transaction for scheduling (Pack skipped the transaction because of account conflicts using the full slow check) |
| pack\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãschedule  <br>{pack\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãschedule="defer\_‚Äãskip"} | counter | Result of trying to consider a transaction for scheduling (Pack skipped the transaction it previously exceeded the per-account block write cost limit too many times) |
| pack\_‚Äãbundle\_‚Äãcrank\_‚Äãstatus  <br>{bundle\_‚Äãcrank\_‚Äãresult="not\_‚Äãneeded"} | counter | Result of considering whether bundle cranks are needed (On-chain state in the correct state) |
| pack\_‚Äãbundle\_‚Äãcrank\_‚Äãstatus  <br>{bundle\_‚Äãcrank\_‚Äãresult="inserted"} | counter | Result of considering whether bundle cranks are needed (Inserted an initializer bundle to update the on-chain state) |
| pack\_‚Äãbundle\_‚Äãcrank\_‚Äãstatus  <br>{bundle\_‚Äãcrank\_‚Äãresult="creation\_‚Äãfailed"} | counter | Result of considering whether bundle cranks are needed (Tried to insert an initializer bundle to update the on-chain state, but creation failed) |
| pack\_‚Äãbundle\_‚Äãcrank\_‚Äãstatus  <br>{bundle\_‚Äãcrank\_‚Äãresult="insertion\_‚Äãfailed"} | counter | Result of considering whether bundle cranks are needed (Tried to insert an initializer bundle to update the on-chain state, but insertion failed) |
| pack\_‚Äãcus\_‚Äãconsumed\_‚Äãin\_‚Äãblock | gauge | The number of cost units consumed in the current block, or 0 if pack is not currently packing a block |
| pack\_‚Äãcus\_‚Äãscheduled | histogram | The number of cost units scheduled for each block pack produced. This can be higher than the block limit because of returned CUs. |
| pack\_‚Äãcus\_‚Äãrebated | histogram | The number of compute units rebated for each block pack produced. Compute units are rebated when a transaction fails prior to execution or requests more compute units than it uses. |
| pack\_‚Äãcus\_‚Äãnet | histogram | The net number of cost units (scheduled - rebated) in each block pack produced. |
| pack\_‚Äãcus\_‚Äãpct | histogram | The percent of the total block cost limit used for each block pack produced. |
| pack\_‚Äãdelete\_‚Äãmissed | counter | Count of attempts to delete a transaction that wasn't found |
| pack\_‚Äãdelete\_‚Äãhit | counter | Count of attempts to delete a transaction that was found and deleted |

Execle Tile [‚Äã](https://docs.firedancer.io/api/metrics.html#execle-tile)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Metric | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="success"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction executed successfully) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="instructon\_‚Äãerror"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (An error occurred while processing an instruction) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="account\_‚Äãnot\_‚Äãfound"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction fee payer address was not found) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="program\_‚Äãaccount\_‚Äãnot\_‚Äãfound"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (A program account referenced by the transaction was not found) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="insufficient\_‚Äãfunds\_‚Äãfor\_‚Äãfee"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction fee payer did not have balance to pay the fee) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="invalid\_‚Äãaccount\_‚Äãfor\_‚Äãfee"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction fee payer account is not owned by the system program, or has data that is not a nonce) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="already\_‚Äãprocessed"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction has already been processed in a recent block) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="blockhash\_‚Äãnot\_‚Äãfound"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction references a blockhash that is not recent, or advances a nonce with the wrong value) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="invalid\_‚Äãprogram\_‚Äãfor\_‚Äãexecution"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (A program account referenced by the transaction was no executable. TODO: No longer needed with SIMD-0162) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="address\_‚Äãlookup\_‚Äãtable\_‚Äãnot\_‚Äãfound"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction references an ALUT account that does not exist or is inactive) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="invalid\_‚Äãaddress\_‚Äãlookup\_‚Äãtable\_‚Äãowner"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction references an ALUT account that is not owned by the ALUT program account) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="invalid\_‚Äãaddress\_‚Äãlookup\_‚Äãtable\_‚Äãdata"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction references an ALUT account that contains data which is not a valid ALUT) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="invalid\_‚Äãaddress\_‚Äãlookup\_‚Äãtable\_‚Äãindex"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction references an account offset from the ALUT which does not exist) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="max\_‚Äãloaded\_‚Äãaccounts\_‚Äãdata\_‚Äãsize\_‚Äãexceeded"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The total account data size of the loaded accounts exceeds the consensus limit) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="duplicate\_‚Äãinstruction"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (A compute budget program instruction was invoked more than once) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="invalid\_‚Äãloaded\_‚Äãaccounts\_‚Äãdata\_‚Äãsize\_‚Äãlimit"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The compute budget program was invoked and set the loaded accounts data size to zero) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="nonce\_‚Äãalready\_‚Äãadvanced"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction references a nonce account that is already advanced) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="nonce\_‚Äãadvance\_‚Äãfailed"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction is a nonce transaction but the advance instruction was not valid or failed) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="nonce\_‚Äãwrong\_‚Äãblockhash"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction is a nonce transaction but the blockhash is not the correct one) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="account\_‚Äãin\_‚Äãuse"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction conflicts with another transaction in the microblock. TODO: No longer possible with smart dispatcher) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="account\_‚Äãloaded\_‚Äãtwice"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction references the same account twice) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="signature\_‚Äãfailure"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction had an invalid signature) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="too\_‚Äãmany\_‚Äãaccount\_‚Äãlocks"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction references too many accounts. TODO: No longer possible with smart dispatcher) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="insufficient\_‚Äãfunds\_‚Äãfor\_‚Äãrent"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction would leave an account with a lower balance than the rent-exempt minimum) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="unbalanced\_‚Äãtransaction"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The total referenced account lamports before and after the transaction was unbalanced) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãresult="bundle\_‚Äãpeer"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The transaction was part of a bundle and an earlier transaction in the bundle failed) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãlanded  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãlanded="landed\_‚Äãsuccess"} | counter | Whether a transaction landed in the block or not (Transaction landed) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãlanded  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãlanded="landed\_‚Äãfees\_‚Äãonly"} | counter | Whether a transaction landed in the block or not (Transaction landed, but was fees only and did not execute) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãlanded  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãlanded="landed\_‚Äãfailed"} | counter | Whether a transaction landed in the block or not (Transaction landed, but failed to execute) |
| execle\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãlanded  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãlanded="unlanded"} | counter | Whether a transaction landed in the block or not (Transaction did not land) |
| execle\_‚Äãcompute\_‚Äãunits\_‚Äãtotal | counter | Estimated number of compute units executed since tile start |

Shred Tile [‚Äã](https://docs.firedancer.io/api/metrics.html#shred-tile)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Metric | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| shred\_‚Äãcluster\_‚Äãcontact\_‚Äãinfo\_‚Äãcnt | histogram | Number of contact infos in the cluster contact info message |
| shred\_‚Äãmicroblocks\_‚Äãabandoned | counter | The number of microblocks that were abandoned because we switched slots without finishing the current slot |
| shred\_‚Äãinvalid\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãid | counter | The number of times a block was created with unknown parent block\_id |
| shred\_‚Äãbatch\_‚Äãsz | histogram | The size (in bytes) of each microblock batch that is shredded |
| shred\_‚Äãbatch\_‚Äãmicroblock\_‚Äãcnt | histogram | The number of microblocks in each microblock batch that is shredded |
| shred\_‚Äãshredding\_‚Äãduration\_‚Äãseconds | histogram | Duration of producing one FEC set from the shredder |
| shred\_‚Äãadd\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãduration\_‚Äãseconds | histogram | Duration of verifying and processing one shred received from the network |
| shred\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãprocessed  <br>{shred\_‚Äãprocessing\_‚Äãresult="bad\_‚Äãslot"} | counter | The result of processing a shred from the network (Shred was for a slot for which we don't know the leader) |
| shred\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãprocessed  <br>{shred\_‚Äãprocessing\_‚Äãresult="parse\_‚Äãfailed"} | counter | The result of processing a shred from the network (Shred parsing failed) |
| shred\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãprocessed  <br>{shred\_‚Äãprocessing\_‚Äãresult="equivoc"} | counter | The result of processing a shred from the network (Shred was equivocated with another shred) |
| shred\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãprocessed  <br>{shred\_‚Äãprocessing\_‚Äãresult="rejected"} | counter | The result of processing a shred from the network (Shred was invalid for one of many reasons) |
| shred\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãprocessed  <br>{shred\_‚Äãprocessing\_‚Äãresult="ignored"} | counter | The result of processing a shred from the network (Shred was ignored because we had already reconstructed the FEC set, or was for an old slot) |
| shred\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãprocessed  <br>{shred\_‚Äãprocessing\_‚Äãresult="duplicate"} | counter | The result of processing a shred from the network (Shred was a duplicate of a previously received valid shred of an incomplete FEC set) |
| shred\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãprocessed  <br>{shred\_‚Äãprocessing\_‚Äãresult="okay"} | counter | The result of processing a shred from the network (Shred accepted to an incomplete FEC set) |
| shred\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãprocessed  <br>{shred\_‚Äãprocessing\_‚Äãresult="completes"} | counter | The result of processing a shred from the network (Shred accepted and resulted in a valid, complete FEC set) |
| shred\_‚Äãfec\_‚Äãset\_‚Äãspilled | counter | The number of FEC sets that were spilled because they didn't complete in time and we needed space |
| shred\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãrejected\_‚Äãinitial | counter | The number of shreds that were rejected before any resources were allocated for the FEC set |
| shred\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãrejected\_‚Äãunchained | counter | The number of shreds that were rejected because they're not chained merkle shreds |
| shred\_‚Äãfec\_‚Äãrejected\_‚Äãfatal | counter | The number of FEC sets that were rejected for reasons that cause the whole FEC set to become invalid |
| shred\_‚Äãbad\_‚Äãnonce | counter | The number of shreds we received that seemed to be repair responses but had an incorrect nonce |
| shred\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãrepair\_‚Äãrcv | counter | The number of times we received a repair shred |
| shred\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãrepair\_‚Äãrcv\_‚Äãbytes | counter | The number bytes received from network packets with repair shreds. Bytes include network headers |
| shred\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãturbine\_‚Äãrcv | counter | The number of times we received a turbine shred |
| shred\_‚Äãshred\_‚Äãturbine\_‚Äãrcv\_‚Äãbytes | counter | The number bytes received from network packets with turbine shreds. Bytes include network headers |

Gossip Tile [‚Äã](https://docs.firedancer.io/api/metrics.html#gossip-tile)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Metric | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracker\_‚Äãcapacity | counter | The peer tracking capacity of the ping tracker |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracker\_‚Äãcount  <br>{ping\_‚Äãtracked\_‚Äãtype="unpinged"} | gauge | The number of peers being tracked for ping/pong (Peer is known but has not been pinged yet) |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracker\_‚Äãcount  <br>{ping\_‚Äãtracked\_‚Äãtype="invalid"} | gauge | The number of peers being tracked for ping/pong (Peer was pinged but has not yet responded, or responded with an invalid pong) |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracker\_‚Äãcount  <br>{ping\_‚Äãtracked\_‚Äãtype="valid"} | gauge | The number of peers being tracked for ping/pong (Peer was pinged and is currently valid) |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracker\_‚Äãcount  <br>{ping\_‚Äãtracked\_‚Äãtype="valid\_‚Äãrefreshing"} | gauge | The number of peers being tracked for ping/pong (Peer was pinged and is currently valid, and is being refreshed with a new ping) |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracker\_‚Äãpong\_‚Äãresult  <br>{pong\_‚Äãresponse="staked"} | counter | The result of processing a pong response to a ping (Pong ignored as node is staked) |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracker\_‚Äãpong\_‚Äãresult  <br>{pong\_‚Äãresponse="entrypoint"} | counter | The result of processing a pong response to a ping (Pong ignored as node is an entrypoint) |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracker\_‚Äãpong\_‚Äãresult  <br>{pong\_‚Äãresponse="untracked"} | counter | The result of processing a pong response to a ping (Pong ignored as node has no outstanding ping) |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracker\_‚Äãpong\_‚Äãresult  <br>{pong\_‚Äãresponse="address"} | counter | The result of processing a pong response to a ping (Pong ignored as responding node doesn't match pinged address) |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracker\_‚Äãpong\_‚Äãresult  <br>{pong\_‚Äãresponse="token"} | counter | The result of processing a pong response to a ping (Pong ignored as token was not valid) |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracker\_‚Äãpong\_‚Äãresult  <br>{pong\_‚Äãresponse="success"} | counter | The result of processing a pong response to a ping (Pong accepted) |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracker\_‚Äãevicted\_‚Äãcount | counter | The number of peers evicted from the ping tracker to make space for new peers |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracked\_‚Äãcount | counter | The total number of peers ever tracked for ping/pong |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracker\_‚Äãstake\_‚Äãchanged\_‚Äãcount | counter | The number of times a tracked peer was removed from tracking as it became staked |
| gossip\_‚Äãping\_‚Äãtracker\_‚Äãaddress\_‚Äãchanged\_‚Äãcount | counter | The number of times a tracked peer was removed from tracking as it's gossip address changed |
| gossip\_‚Äãcrds\_‚Äãcapacity | gauge | The capacity of the data store |
| gossip\_‚Äãcrds\_‚Äãcount  <br>{crds\_‚Äãvalue="contact\_‚Äãinfo\_‚Äãv1"} | gauge | The number of entries in the data store (Contact Info V1) |
| gossip\_‚Äãcrds\_‚Äãcount  <br>{crds\_‚Äãvalue="vote"} | gauge | The number of entries in the data store (Vote) |
| gossip\_‚Äãcrds\_‚Äãcount  <br>{crds\_‚Äãvalue="lowest\_‚Äãslot"} | gauge | The number of entries in the data store (Lowest Slot) |
| gossip\_‚Äãcrds\_‚Äãcount  <br>{crds\_‚Äãvalue="snapshot\_‚Äãhashes"} | gauge | The number of entries in the data store (Snapshot Hashes) |
| gossip\_‚Äãcrds\_‚Äãcount  <br>{crds\_‚Äãvalue="accounts\_‚Äãhashes"} | gauge | The number of entries in the data store (Accounts Hashes) |
| gossip\_‚Äãcrds\_‚Äãcount  <br>{crds\_‚Äãvalue="epoch\_‚Äãslots"} | gauge | The number of entries in the data store (Epoch Slots) |
| gossip\_‚Äãcrds\_‚Äãcount  <br>{crds\_‚Äãvalue="version\_‚Äãv1"} | gauge | The number of entries in the data store (Version V1) |
| gossip\_‚Äãcrds\_‚Äãcount  <br>{crds\_‚Äãvalue="version\_‚Äãv2"} | gauge | The number of entries in the data store (Version V2) |
| gossip\_‚Äãcrds\_‚Äãcount  <br>{crds\_‚Äãvalue="node\_‚Äãinstance"} | gauge | The number of entries in the data store (Node Instance) |
| gossip\_‚Äãcrds\_‚Äãcount  <br>{crds\_‚Äãvalue="duplicate\_‚Äãshred"} | gauge | The number of entries in the data store (Duplicate Shred) |
| gossip\_‚Äãcrds\_‚Äãcount  <br>{crds\_‚Äãvalue="incremental\_‚Äãsnapshot\_‚Äãhashes"} | gauge | The number of entries in the data store (Incremental Snapshot Hashes) |
| gossip\_‚Äãcrds\_‚Äãcount  <br>{crds\_‚Äãvalue="contact\_‚Äãinfo\_‚Äãv2"} | gauge | The number of entries in the data store (Contact Info V2) |

Repair Tile [‚Äã](https://docs.firedancer.io/api/metrics.html#repair-tile)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Metric | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| repair\_‚Äãtotal\_‚Äãpkt\_‚Äãcount | counter | How many network packets we have sent, including reqs, pings, pongs, etc |
| repair\_‚Äãsent\_‚Äãpkt\_‚Äãtypes  <br>{repair\_‚Äãsent\_‚Äãrequest\_‚Äãtypes="needed\_‚Äãwindow"} | counter | What types of client messages are we sending (Need Window) |
| repair\_‚Äãsent\_‚Äãpkt\_‚Äãtypes  <br>{repair\_‚Äãsent\_‚Äãrequest\_‚Äãtypes="needed\_‚Äãhighest\_‚Äãwindow"} | counter | What types of client messages are we sending (Need Highest Window) |
| repair\_‚Äãsent\_‚Äãpkt\_‚Äãtypes  <br>{repair\_‚Äãsent\_‚Äãrequest\_‚Äãtypes="needed\_‚Äãorphan"} | counter | What types of client messages are we sending (Need Orphans) |
| repair\_‚Äãsent\_‚Äãpkt\_‚Äãtypes  <br>{repair\_‚Äãsent\_‚Äãrequest\_‚Äãtypes="pong"} | counter | What types of client messages are we sending (Pong) |
| repair\_‚Äãrepaired\_‚Äãslots | counter | Until which slots have we fully repaired |
| repair\_‚Äãcurrent\_‚Äãslot | counter | Our view of the current cluster slot, max slot received |
| repair\_‚Äãrequest\_‚Äãpeers | counter | How many peers have we requested |
| repair\_‚Äãsign\_‚Äãtile\_‚Äãunavail | counter | How many times no sign tiles were available to send request |
| repair\_‚Äãeager\_‚Äãrepair\_‚Äãaggresses | counter | How many times we pass eager repair threshold |
| repair\_‚Äãrerequest\_‚Äãqueue | counter | How many times we re-request a shred from the inflights queue |
| repair\_‚Äãmalformed\_‚Äãping | counter | How many times we received a malformed ping |
| repair\_‚Äãunknown\_‚Äãpeer\_‚Äãping | counter | How many times we received a ping from an unknown peer |
| repair\_‚Äãfailed\_‚Äãsigverify\_‚Äãping | counter | How many times we failed to verify the signature of a ping |
| repair\_‚Äãslot\_‚Äãcomplete\_‚Äãtime | histogram | Time in seconds it took to complete a slot |
| repair\_‚Äãresponse\_‚Äãlatency | histogram | Time in nanoseconds it took to receive a repair request response |
| repair\_‚Äãsign\_‚Äãduration\_‚Äãseconds | histogram | Duration of signing a message |
| repair\_‚Äãblk\_‚Äãevicted | counter | How many times we evicted a block from the forest |
| repair\_‚Äãblk\_‚Äãfailed\_‚Äãinsert | counter | How many times we failed to insert a block into the forest due to failed eviction |

Replay Tile [‚Äã](https://docs.firedancer.io/api/metrics.html#replay-tile)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Metric | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| replay\_‚Äãstore\_‚Äãquery\_‚Äãacquire | counter | Count of store slock acquires for query |
| replay\_‚Äãstore\_‚Äãquery\_‚Äãrelease | counter | Count of store slock releases for query |
| replay\_‚Äãstore\_‚Äãquery\_‚Äãwait | histogram | Time in seconds spent waiting to acquire the slock for query |
| replay\_‚Äãstore\_‚Äãquery\_‚Äãwork | histogram | Time in seconds spent working before releasing the slock for query |
| replay\_‚Äãstore\_‚Äãquery\_‚Äãcnt | counter | Count of queries |
| replay\_‚Äãstore\_‚Äãquery\_‚Äãmissing\_‚Äãcnt | counter | Count of queries where merkle root was missing |
| replay\_‚Äãstore\_‚Äãquery\_‚Äãmr | gauge | First 8 bytes of most recently queried merkle root |
| replay\_‚Äãstore\_‚Äãquery\_‚Äãmissing\_‚Äãmr | gauge | First 8 bytes of most recently queried missing merkle root |
| replay\_‚Äãroot\_‚Äãslot | gauge | The slot at which our node has most recently rooted |
| replay\_‚Äãroot\_‚Äãdistance | gauge | The distance in slots between our current root and the current reset slot |
| replay\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãslot | gauge | The slot at which we are currently leader, or 0 if none |
| replay\_‚Äãnext\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãslot | gauge | The slot at which we are next leader, or 0 if none. If we are currently leader, this is the same as the current leader slot |
| replay\_‚Äãreset\_‚Äãslot | gauge | The slot at which we last reset the replay stage, or 0 if unknown |
| replay\_‚Äãmax\_‚Äãlive\_‚Äãbanks | gauge | The maximum number of banks we can have alive |
| replay\_‚Äãlive\_‚Äãbanks | gauge | The number of banks we currently have alive |
| replay\_‚Äãreasm\_‚Äãfree | gauge | The number of free FEC sets in the reassembly queue |
| replay\_‚Äãreasm\_‚Äãlatest\_‚Äãslot | gauge | Slot of the latest FEC set in the reassembly queue that can be replayed |
| replay\_‚Äãreasm\_‚Äãlatest\_‚Äãfec\_‚Äãidx | gauge | FEC set index of the latest FEC set in the reassembly queue that can be replayed |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãactive\_‚Äãbank\_‚Äãidx | gauge | The bank that the replay scheduler is currently dispatching work for |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãlast\_‚Äãdispatch\_‚Äãbank\_‚Äãidx | gauge | The bank that the replay scheduler last dispatched work for |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãlast\_‚Äãdispatch\_‚Äãtime\_‚Äãnanos | gauge | Timestamp when the replay scheduler last dispatched work |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãstaging\_‚Äãlane\_‚Äãpopcnt | gauge | The total number of staging lanes that are currently occupied in the replay scheduler. Up to four staging lanes can be occupied at once |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãstaging\_‚Äãlane\_‚Äãpopcnt\_‚Äãwmk | gauge | The high watermark number of staging lanes that were at one point occupied in the replay scheduler |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãstaging\_‚Äãlane\_‚Äãhead\_‚Äãbank\_‚Äãidx0 | gauge | The bank at the head of staging lane 0 of the replay dispatcher |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãstaging\_‚Äãlane\_‚Äãhead\_‚Äãbank\_‚Äãidx1 | gauge | The bank at the head of staging lane 1 of the replay dispatcher |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãstaging\_‚Äãlane\_‚Äãhead\_‚Äãbank\_‚Äãidx2 | gauge | The bank at the head of staging lane 2 of the replay dispatcher |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãstaging\_‚Äãlane\_‚Äãhead\_‚Äãbank\_‚Äãidx3 | gauge | The bank at the head of staging lane 3 of the replay dispatcher |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãpool\_‚Äãpopcnt | gauge | The total number of transactions that are available to be scheduled in the replay scheduler |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãpool\_‚Äãsize | gauge | The maximum number of transactions that the replay scheduler can consider. This value is fixed at Firedancer startup but is a useful reference for TxnPoolPopcnt |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãmblk\_‚Äãpool\_‚Äãpopcnt | gauge | The total number of microblocks that are available to be scheduled in the replay scheduler |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãmblk\_‚Äãpool\_‚Äãsize | gauge | The maximum number of microblocks that the replay scheduler can consider. This value is fixed at Firedancer startup but is a useful reference for MblkPoolPopcnt |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãpool\_‚Äãpopcnt | gauge | The total number of blocks that are alive in the replay scheduler |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãpool\_‚Äãsize | gauge | The maximum number of blocks that the replay scheduler can keep track of. This value is fixed at Firedancer startup but is a useful reference for BlockPoolPopcnt |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãadded\_‚Äãstaged | counter | Blocks added to the replay scheduler as staged |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãadded\_‚Äãunstaged | counter | Blocks added to the replay scheduler as unstaged |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãreplayed | counter | Blocks that the replay scheduler considers fully replayed |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãabandoned | counter | Blocks that the replay scheduler abandoned for any reason |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãbad | counter | Blocks that the replay scheduler considers bad |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãpromoted | counter | Blocks that the replay scheduler promoted from unstaged to a staging lane |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãdemoted | counter | Blocks that the replay scheduler demoted from a staging lane to unstaged |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãdeactivate\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãchild | counter | Number of times that the replay scheduler stopped dispatching because a block fully replayed and there was no child block available yet |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãdeactivate\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãwork | counter | Number of times that the replay scheduler stopped dispatching because a partially replayed block ran out of work to dispatch |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãdeactivate\_‚Äãabandoned | counter | Number of times that the replay scheduler stopped dispatching because a block got abandoned for any reason |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãdeactivate\_‚Äãminority | counter | Number of times that the replay scheduler stopped dispatching because a block got abandoned for being on a minority fork |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãlane\_‚Äãswitch | counter | Number of times that the replay scheduler switched the lane that it is dispatching from |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãlane\_‚Äãpromote | counter | Number of times that the replay scheduler promoted one or more blocks onto a staging lane |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãlane\_‚Äãdemote | counter | Number of times that the replay scheduler demoted one or more blocks from a staging lane |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãfork\_‚Äãobserved | counter | Number of forks that the replay scheduler has observed |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãalut\_‚Äãsuccess | counter | Number of transactions with address lookup tables that the replay scheduler successfully expanded |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãalut\_‚Äãfailure | counter | Number of transactions with address lookup tables that the replay scheduler failed to expand |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãabandoned\_‚Äãparsed | counter | Number of transactions that were parsed but ended up being in abandoned blocks |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãabandoned\_‚Äãexec | counter | Number of transactions that were executed but ended up being in abandoned blocks |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãabandoned\_‚Äãdone | counter | Number of transactions that were fully replayed but ended up being in abandoned blocks |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãweighted\_‚Äãin\_‚Äãflight | counter | Cumulative number of transactions that have been in-flight from the replay scheduler's point of view, weighted by the duration of each transaction. This value is useful as the dividend for TxnWeightedInFlightDuration |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãweighted\_‚Äãin\_‚Äãflight\_‚Äãduration | counter | Duration over which TxnWeightedInFlight was accumulated. Use this as divisor to get the average number of in-flight transactions |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãnone\_‚Äãin\_‚Äãflight\_‚Äãduration | counter | Duration over which the replay scheduler had no transaction in-flight. This value is useful in a ratio against WeightedInFlightDuration to see how often the replay transaction execution pipeline was idle |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãparsed | counter | Number of transactions that the replay pipeline has parsed |
| replay\_‚Äãsched\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãexec | counter | Number of transactions that the replay pipeline has executed |

| Metric | Type | Description |

| tower\_‚Äãroot\_‚Äãslot | gauge | Root slot |
| tower\_‚Äãinit\_‚Äãslot | gauge | Init slot |

| tower\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãbad\_‚Äãdeser | counter | Vote txn failed to deserialize |

| tower\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãnot\_‚Äãtower\_‚Äãsync | counter | Vote txn was not a TowerSync instruction |
| tower\_‚Äãtxn\_‚Äãempty\_‚Äãtower | counter | Vote txn had an empty tower (validator hasn't voted) |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãsuccess\_‚Äãmerkle | counter | Merkle root conflict |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãsuccess\_‚Äãmeta | counter | Coding metadata conflict |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãsuccess\_‚Äãlast | counter | Last shred index conflict |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãsuccess\_‚Äãoverlap | counter | Overlapping FEC set conflict |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãsuccess\_‚Äãchained | counter | Chained merkle root conflict |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãerr\_‚Äãserde | counter | Invalid serialization |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãerr\_‚Äãslot | counter | Shreds were for different slots |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãerr\_‚Äãversion | counter | Either shred had wrong shred version |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãerr\_‚Äãtype | counter | Wrong shred type (must be chained merkle) |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãerr\_‚Äãmerkle | counter | Failed to derive merkle root |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãerr\_‚Äãsignature | counter | Failed to sig verify |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãerr\_‚Äãchunk\_‚Äãcnt | counter | num\_chunks != FD\_EQVOC\_CHUNK\_CNT |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãerr\_‚Äãchunk\_‚Äãidx | counter | chunk\_index >= FD\_EQVOC\_CHUNK\_CNT |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãerr\_‚Äãchunk\_‚Äãlen | counter | chunk\_len does not match expected length for chunk\_index |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãerr\_‚Äãignored\_‚Äãfrom | counter | Unrecognized from address |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãerr\_‚Äãignored\_‚Äãslot | counter | Slot older than root or unable to derive leader schedule |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãproof\_‚Äãconstructed | counter | Number of duplicate proofs we constructed from shreds |
| tower\_‚Äãeqvoc\_‚Äãproof\_‚Äãverified | counter | Number of duplicate proofs we verified from gossip |
| tower\_‚Äãghost\_‚Äãnot\_‚Äãvoted | counter | Ghost vote skipped because voter hasn't voted |
| tower\_‚Äãghost\_‚Äãtoo\_‚Äãold | counter | Ghost vote slot was behind the root |
| tower\_‚Äãghost\_‚Äãalready\_‚Äãvoted | counter | Ghost vote slot was not newer than previous vote |
| tower\_‚Äãhfork\_‚Äãunknown\_‚Äãvtr | counter | Hfork voter not in voter set |
| tower\_‚Äãhfork\_‚Äãalready\_‚Äãvoted | counter | Hfork voter already voted for this block\_id |
| tower\_‚Äãhfork\_‚Äãtoo\_‚Äãold | counter | Hfork vote slot not newer than previous |
| tower\_‚Äãhfork\_‚Äãmatched\_‚Äãslot | gauge | Highest slot where 52%+ of stake agreed on our bank hash |
| tower\_‚Äãhfork\_‚Äãmismatched\_‚Äãslot | gauge | Highest slot where 52%+ of stake agreed on a different bank hash than ours (we hard forked) |
| tower\_‚Äãancestor\_‚Äãrollback | counter | Rollback to an ancestor of our prev vote (can't vote) |
| tower\_‚Äãsibling\_‚Äãconfirmed | counter | Duplicate sibling got confirmed (can't vote) |
| tower\_‚Äãsame\_‚Äãfork | counter | Same fork as prev vote (can vote) |
| tower\_‚Äãswitch\_‚Äãpass | counter | Prev vote was on a different fork, but we are allowed to switch (can vote) |
| tower\_‚Äãswitch\_‚Äãfail | counter | Prev vote was on a different fork, and we are not allowed to switch (can't vote) |
| tower\_‚Äãlockout\_‚Äãfail | counter | Locked out (can't vote) |
| tower\_‚Äãthreshold\_‚Äãfail | counter | Did not pass threshold check (can't vote) |
| tower\_‚Äãpropagated\_‚Äãfail | counter | Prev leader block did not propagate (can't vote) |
| tower\_‚Äãvotes\_‚Äãtoo\_‚Äãold | counter | Vote slot was behind the votes root |
| tower\_‚Äãvotes\_‚Äãtoo\_‚Äãnew | counter | Vote slot was too far ahead of the votes root |
| tower\_‚Äãvotes\_‚Äãunknown\_‚Äãvtr | counter | Vote account was not in the voter set |
| tower\_‚Äãvotes\_‚Äãalready\_‚Äãvoted | counter | Voter already voted for this slot |
| tower\_‚Äãvotes\_‚Äãunknown\_‚Äãslot | counter | Vote txn was for a slot we haven't replayed |
| tower\_‚Äãvotes\_‚Äãunknown\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãid | counter | Vote txn was for a block id we don't recognize |

Diag Tile [‚Äã](https://docs.firedancer.io/api/metrics.html#diag-tile)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Metric | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| diag\_‚Äãbundle\_‚Äãhealth | gauge | 0=unhealthy, 1=healthy, 2=disabled. A healthy bundle subsystem means at least one bundle tile currently zhas an active connection to the block engine server |
| diag\_‚Äãvote\_‚Äãhealth | gauge | 0=unhealthy, 1=healthy, 2=disabled. A healthy vote subsystem means the client has cast at least one vote in both the last 60 seconds and last 150 slots (before the currently replay slot) |
| diag\_‚Äãreplay\_‚Äãhealth | gauge | 0=unhealthy, 1=healthy, 2=disabled. A healthy replay subsystem means that the largest fully-processed replay slot on the chosen consensus fork is within 12 slots of the current turbine slot |
| diag\_‚Äãturbine\_‚Äãhealth | gauge | 0=unhealthy, 1=healthy, 2=disabled. A healthy turbine subsystem means that the largest slot associated with received turbine shreds has not stalled for 12 seconds, and also that the average replay ingress traffic exceeds the average ingress repair traffic over the past 12 seconds |

| Metric | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| event\_‚Äãconnection\_‚Äãstate | gauge | 0 = disconnected, 1 = connecting, 2 = connected |

| event\_‚Äãevent\_‚Äãqueue\_‚Äãdrops | counter | The total number of events dropped because the event queue was full |
| event\_‚Äãevent\_‚Äãqueue\_‚Äãbytes\_‚Äãused | gauge | The current number of bytes used in the event queue |
| event\_‚Äãevent\_‚Äãqueue\_‚Äãbytes\_‚Äãcapacity | gauge | The total capacity in bytes of the event queue |
| event\_‚Äãevents\_‚Äãsent | counter | The total number of events sent to the event service |
| event\_‚Äãevents\_‚Äãacked | counter | The total number of events acknowledged by the event service |
| event\_‚Äãbytes\_‚Äãwritten | counter | The total number of bytes written to the event service |
| event\_‚Äãbytes\_‚Äãread | counter | The total number of bytes read from the event service |

Resolh Tile [‚Äã](https://docs.firedancer.io/api/metrics.html#resolh-tile)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Metric | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| resolh\_‚Äãno\_‚Äãbank\_‚Äãdrop | counter | Count of transactions dropped because the bank was not available |
| resolh\_‚Äãstash\_‚Äãoperation  <br>{resolve\_‚Äãstash\_‚Äãoperation="inserted"} | counter | Count of operations that happened on the transaction stash (A transaction with an unknown blockhash was added to the stash) |
| resolh\_‚Äãstash\_‚Äãoperation  <br>{resolve\_‚Äãstash\_‚Äãoperation="overrun"} | counter | Count of operations that happened on the transaction stash (A transaction with an unknown blockhash was dropped because the stash was full) |
| resolh\_‚Äãstash\_‚Äãoperation  <br>{resolve\_‚Äãstash\_‚Äãoperation="published"} | counter | Count of operations that happened on the transaction stash (A transaction with an unknown blockhash was published as the blockhash became known) |
| resolh\_‚Äãstash\_‚Äãoperation  <br>{resolve\_‚Äãstash\_‚Äãoperation="removed"} | counter | Count of operations that happened on the transaction stash (A transaction with an unknown blockhash was removed from the stash without publishing, due to a bad LUT resolved failure, or no bank. These errors are double counted with the respective metrics for those categories) |
| resolh\_‚Äãlut\_‚Äãresolved  <br>{lut\_‚Äãresolve\_‚Äãresult="invalid\_‚Äãlookup\_‚Äãindex"} | counter | Count of address lookup tables resolved (The transaction referenced an index in a LUT that didn't exist) |
| resolh\_‚Äãlut\_‚Äãresolved  <br>{lut\_‚Äãresolve\_‚Äãresult="account\_‚Äãuninitialized"} | counter | Count of address lookup tables resolved (The account referenced as a LUT hasn't been initialized) |
| resolh\_‚Äãlut\_‚Äãresolved  <br>{lut\_‚Äãresolve\_‚Äãresult="invalid\_‚Äãaccount\_‚Äãdata"} | counter | Count of address lookup tables resolved (The account referenced as a LUT couldn't be parsed) |
| resolh\_‚Äãlut\_‚Äãresolved  <br>{lut\_‚Äãresolve\_‚Äãresult="invalid\_‚Äãaccount\_‚Äãowner"} | counter | Count of address lookup tables resolved (The account referenced as a LUT wasn't owned by the ALUT program ID) |
| resolh\_‚Äãlut\_‚Äãresolved  <br>{lut\_‚Äãresolve\_‚Äãresult="account\_‚Äãnot\_‚Äãfound"} | counter | Count of address lookup tables resolved (The account referenced as a LUT couldn't be found) |
| resolh\_‚Äãlut\_‚Äãresolved  <br>{lut\_‚Äãresolve\_‚Äãresult="success"} | counter | Count of address lookup tables resolved (Resolved successfully) |
| resolh\_‚Äãblockhash\_‚Äãexpired | counter | Count of transactions that failed to resolve because the blockhash was expired |
| resolh\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãbundle\_‚Äãpeer\_‚Äãfailure | counter | Count of transactions that failed to resolve because a peer transaction in the bundle failed |

Bank Tile [‚Äã](https://docs.firedancer.io/api/metrics.html#bank-tile)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Metric | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãsanitize\_‚Äãfailure | counter | Number of transactions that failed to sanitize |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãnot\_‚Äãexecuted\_‚Äãfailure | counter | Number of transactions that did not execute. This is different than transactions which fail to execute, which make it onto the chain |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãload\_‚Äãaddress\_‚Äãtables  <br>{lut\_‚Äãresolve\_‚Äãresult="invalid\_‚Äãlookup\_‚Äãindex"} | counter | Result of loading address lookup tables for a transaction. If there are multiple errors for the transaction, only the first one is reported (The transaction referenced an index in a LUT that didn't exist) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãload\_‚Äãaddress\_‚Äãtables  <br>{lut\_‚Äãresolve\_‚Äãresult="account\_‚Äãuninitialized"} | counter | Result of loading address lookup tables for a transaction. If there are multiple errors for the transaction, only the first one is reported (The account referenced as a LUT hasn't been initialized) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãload\_‚Äãaddress\_‚Äãtables  <br>{lut\_‚Äãresolve\_‚Äãresult="invalid\_‚Äãaccount\_‚Äãdata"} | counter | Result of loading address lookup tables for a transaction. If there are multiple errors for the transaction, only the first one is reported (The account referenced as a LUT couldn't be parsed) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãload\_‚Äãaddress\_‚Äãtables  <br>{lut\_‚Äãresolve\_‚Äãresult="invalid\_‚Äãaccount\_‚Äãowner"} | counter | Result of loading address lookup tables for a transaction. If there are multiple errors for the transaction, only the first one is reported (The account referenced as a LUT wasn't owned by the ALUT program ID) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãload\_‚Äãaddress\_‚Äãtables  <br>{lut\_‚Äãresolve\_‚Äãresult="account\_‚Äãnot\_‚Äãfound"} | counter | Result of loading address lookup tables for a transaction. If there are multiple errors for the transaction, only the first one is reported (The account referenced as a LUT couldn't be found) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãload\_‚Äãaddress\_‚Äãtables  <br>{lut\_‚Äãresolve\_‚Äãresult="success"} | counter | Result of loading address lookup tables for a transaction. If there are multiple errors for the transaction, only the first one is reported (Resolved successfully) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="success"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Success) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="account\_‚Äãin\_‚Äãuse"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (An account is already being processed in another transaction in a way that does not support parallelism) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="account\_‚Äãloaded\_‚Äãtwice"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (A `Pubkey` appears twice in the transaction's `account_keys`. Instructions can reference `Pubkey`s more than once but the message must contain a list with no duplicate keys) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="account\_‚Äãnot\_‚Äãfound"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Attempt to debit an account but found no record of a prior credit) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="program\_‚Äãaccount\_‚Äãnot\_‚Äãfound"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Attempt to load a program that does not exist) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="insufficient\_‚Äãfunds\_‚Äãfor\_‚Äãfee"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The fee payer `Pubkey` does not have sufficient balance to pay the fee to schedule the transaction) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="invalid\_‚Äãaccount\_‚Äãfor\_‚Äãfee"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (This account may not be used to pay transaction fees) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="already\_‚Äãprocessed"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The bank has seen this transaction before. This can occur under normal operation when a UDP packet is duplicated, as a user error from a client not updating its `recent_blockhash`, or as a double-spend attack) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="blockhash\_‚Äãnot\_‚Äãfound"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The bank has not seen the given `recent_blockhash` or the transaction is too old and the `recent_blockhash` has been discarded) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="instruction\_‚Äãerror"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (An error occurred while processing an instruction) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="call\_‚Äãchain\_‚Äãtoo\_‚Äãdeep"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Loader call chain is too deep) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="missing\_‚Äãsignature\_‚Äãfor\_‚Äãfee"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction requires a fee but has no signature present) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="invalid\_‚Äãaccount\_‚Äãindex"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction contains an invalid account reference) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="signature\_‚Äãfailure"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction did not pass signature verification) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="invalid\_‚Äãprogram\_‚Äãfor\_‚Äãexecution"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (This program may not be used for executing instructions) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="sanitize\_‚Äãfailure"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction failed to sanitize accounts offsets correctly implies that account locks are not taken for this TX, and should not be unlocked) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="cluster\_‚Äãmaintenance"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transactions are currently disabled due to cluster maintenance) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="account\_‚Äãborrow\_‚Äãoutstanding"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction processing left an account with an outstanding borrowed reference) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="would\_‚Äãexceed\_‚Äãmax\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãcost\_‚Äãlimit"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction would exceed max Block Cost Limit) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="unsupported\_‚Äãversion"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction version is unsupported) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="invalid\_‚Äãwritable\_‚Äãaccount"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction loads a writable account that cannot be written) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="would\_‚Äãexceed\_‚Äãmax\_‚Äãaccount\_‚Äãcost\_‚Äãlimit"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction would exceed max account limit within the block) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="would\_‚Äãexceed\_‚Äãaccount\_‚Äãdata\_‚Äãblock\_‚Äãlimit"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction would exceed account data limit within the block) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="too\_‚Äãmany\_‚Äãaccount\_‚Äãlocks"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction locked too many accounts) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="address\_‚Äãlookup\_‚Äãtable\_‚Äãnot\_‚Äãfound"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Address lookup table not found) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="invalid\_‚Äãaddress\_‚Äãlookup\_‚Äãtable\_‚Äãowner"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Attempted to lookup addresses from an account owned by the wrong program) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="invalid\_‚Äãaddress\_‚Äãlookup\_‚Äãtable\_‚Äãdata"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Attempted to lookup addresses from an invalid account) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="invalid\_‚Äãaddress\_‚Äãlookup\_‚Äãtable\_‚Äãindex"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Address table lookup uses an invalid index) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="invalid\_‚Äãrent\_‚Äãpaying\_‚Äãaccount"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction leaves an account with a lower balance than rent-exempt minimum) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="would\_‚Äãexceed\_‚Äãmax\_‚Äãvote\_‚Äãcost\_‚Äãlimit"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction would exceed max Vote Cost Limit) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="would\_‚Äãexceed\_‚Äãaccount\_‚Äãdata\_‚Äãtotal\_‚Äãlimit"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction would exceed total account data limit) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="duplicate\_‚Äãinstruction"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction contains a duplicate instruction that is not allowed) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="insufficient\_‚Äãfunds\_‚Äãfor\_‚Äãrent"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction results in an account with insufficient funds for rent) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="max\_‚Äãloaded\_‚Äãaccounts\_‚Äãdata\_‚Äãsize\_‚Äãexceeded"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction exceeded max loaded accounts data size cap) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="invalid\_‚Äãloaded\_‚Äãaccounts\_‚Äãdata\_‚Äãsize\_‚Äãlimit"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (LoadedAccountsDataSizeLimit set for transaction must be greater than 0) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="resanitization\_‚Äãneeded"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Sanitized transaction differed before/after feature activation. Needs to be resanitized) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="program\_‚Äãexecution\_‚Äãtemporarily\_‚Äãrestricted"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Program execution is temporarily restricted on an account) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="unbalanced\_‚Äãtransaction"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The total balance before the transaction does not equal the total balance after the transaction) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="program\_‚Äãcache\_‚Äãhit\_‚Äãmax\_‚Äãlimit"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The total program cache size hit the maximum allowed limit) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="commit\_‚Äãcancelled"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (The process for committing the transaction was cancelled internally) |
| bank\_‚Äãtransaction\_‚Äãresult  <br>{transaction\_‚Äãerror="bundle\_‚Äãpeer"} | counter | Result of loading and executing a transaction (Transaction is part of a bundle and one of the peer transactions failed) |
| bank\_‚Äãprocessing\_‚Äãfailed | counter | Count of transactions for which the processing stage failed and won't land on chain |
| bank\_‚Äãfee\_‚Äãonly\_‚Äãtransactions | counter | Count of transactions that will land on chain but without executing |
| bank\_‚Äãexecuted\_‚Äãfailed\_‚Äãtransactions | counter | Count of transactions that execute on chain but failed |
| bank\_‚Äãsuccessful\_‚Äãtransactions | counter | Count of transactions that execute on chain and succeed |
| bank\_‚Äãcost\_‚Äãmodel\_‚Äãundercount | counter | Count of transactions that used more CUs than the cost model should have permitted them to |

Pohh Tile [‚Äã](https://docs.firedancer.io/api/metrics.html#pohh-tile)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

| Metric | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| pohh\_‚Äãbegin\_‚Äãleader\_‚Äãdelay\_‚Äãseconds | histogram | Delay between when we become leader in a slot and when we receive the bank. |
| pohh\_‚Äãfirst\_‚Äãmicroblock\_‚Äãdelay\_‚Äãseconds | histogram | Delay between when we become leader in a slot and when we receive the first microblock. |
| pohh\_‚Äãslot\_‚Äãdone\_‚Äãdelay\_‚Äãseconds | histogram | Delay between when we become leader in a slot and when we finish the slot. |
| pohh\_‚Äãbundle\_‚Äãinitialize\_‚Äãdelay\_‚Äãseconds | histogram | Delay in starting the slot caused by loading the information needed to generate the bundle crank transactions |

Store Tile [‚Äã](https://docs.firedancer.io/api/metrics.html#store-tile)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Metric | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| store\_‚Äãtransactions\_‚Äãinserted | counter | Count of transactions produced while we were leader in the shreds that have been inserted so far |

Backt Tile [‚Äã](https://docs.firedancer.io/api/metrics.html#backt-tile)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| Metric | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| backt\_‚Äãfinal\_‚Äãslot | gauge | The slot after which the backtest will complete |
| backt\_‚Äãstart\_‚Äãslot | gauge | The slot at which the backtest started |

Benchs Tile [‚Äã](https://docs.firedancer.io/api/metrics.html#benchs-tile)

| Metric | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| benchs\_‚Äãtransactions\_‚Äãsent | counter | Number of benchmark packets sent |
